`mat4_perspective` is standard OpenGL, but `ExtractFrustumPlanes` expects a Reversed-Z `[0, 1]` matrix. `AliceViewer.cpp` claims a Reversed-Z pipeline, so I'll check its `makeInfiniteReversedZProjRH` to see if that's where the real projection logic is.

`makeInfiniteReversedZProjRH` is definitely Reversed-Z `[0, 1]`, but `TilesetTest.h` is still using the standard `Math::mat4_perspective`. I'll swap that out for `AliceViewer::makeInfiniteReversedZProjRH` in `draw()` to align with the pipeline.

Building and rerunning.

Checking logs.

Node 1 is failing the Left plane by a massive margin—over a million units. Something is fundamentally wrong with the coordinate spaces. `mEcefToEnu` should be mapping everything near the origin, but that huge distance suggests it's not. I'll re-examine `Math::denu_matrix` in `AliceMath.h` to see exactly how it's building that ENU rotation and if my translation indices are actually hitting the right spots.

`denu_matrix` is row-major, but `mat4d_mul` is column-major, meaning my `mEcefToEnu` construction is currently mapping ENU to ECEF instead of the other way around. I need to transpose the rotation part: East, North, and Up vectors should be in rows, not columns. My translation calculations are actually correct, so I just need to fix those rotation indices in `TilesetTest.h`.
